Convert an object name into an ASN1_OBJECT if "noname" is not set then search for short and long names first. This will convert the "dotted" form into an object: unlike OBJ_txt2nid it can be used with any objects, not just registered ones.

THIS IS A KLUDGE - Because the _obj is sorted in ASCII order, and I don't have perl (yet), we revert to a LINEAR search when the object wasn't found in the binary search.
